<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">7.9.1.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Compliance with GAAP</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">The individual annual financial statements
(including a balance sheet (<I>Bilanz</I>), profit and loss statement (<I>Gewinn- und Verlustrechnung</I>), notes (<I>Anhang</I>) of the
German Target Group Companies for the financial years ending as of 31&nbsp;December 2024 as attached hereto as <B><U>Schedule&nbsp; 7.9.1</U></B>
(the &ldquo;<B>Financial Statements</B>&rdquo;)</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(i)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">have to the Seller&rsquo;s Best Knowledge been prepared in accordance with the provisions of the German
Commercial Code (<I>HGB</I>) and generally accepted accounting principles (<I>Grunds&auml;tze ordnungsgem&auml;&szlig;er Buchf&uuml;hrung</I>)
and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(ii)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">present, in compliance with these principles, to the Seller&rsquo;s Best Knowledge at the time of preparation
a true and fair view of the net assets, financial position, and results of operations of the German Target Group Companies within the
meaning of Section 264 para 2 of the German Commercial Code (HGB) as of the balance sheet date (<I>Bilanzstichtag</I>).</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">The Parties agree that this Section&nbsp;7.9
shall not qualify as an &ldquo;objective&rdquo; guarantee regarding the financial statements (<I>keine objektive Bilanzgarantie</I>),
but rather as a &ldquo;subjective&rdquo; guarantee regarding the financial statements (<I>subjektive Bilanzgarantie</I>) only. Therefore,
the statements contained in this Section&nbsp;7.9 shall be regarded correct, <I>inter alia</I>, even in the event that any (contingent)
liabilities have not been reflected or provisions have not been recognized in the Financial Statements due to the subjective lack of awareness
or evidence when preparing the Financial Statements (even if, from an objective perspective/in hindsight such liabilities/provisions would
have been required to be reflected in the Financial Statements).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">Further, the Parties agree that the
financial statements as of 31&nbsp;December 2025 will be prepared consistently with the manner and method used to prepare the financial
statements as of 31&nbsp;December 2024, as amended.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(1)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Subject to the provisions contained in this Section&nbsp;8, if and to the extent any Seller&rsquo;s Warranty
under Sec.&nbsp;7.1 to&nbsp;Sec.&nbsp;7.18 is incorrect (&ldquo;<B>Breach</B>&rdquo;), the Seller shall put the Purchaser in such position
as the Purchaser would have been if the Breach had not occurred (restitution in kind &ndash; <I>Naturalrestitution</I>). If the Seller
is unable to achieve such restitution in kind within ten (10) weeks after having received a due Breach Notice by the Purchaser or if such
restitution in kind is impossible or insufficient, then the Purchaser may claim monetary damages (<I>Schadenersatz in Geld</I>).</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(2)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The compensation for damages shall cover only the actual direct damages incurred (<I>unmittelbare Sch&auml;den</I>)
by the Purchaser, provided, however, that the compensation shall specifically not cover and the Purchaser shall not be entitled to claim
compensation for (i) any potential or actual reduction in value (<I>Minderung</I>) of the Inpixon Shares or the Target Group Companies,
(ii) any indirect damages (<I>mittelbare Sch&auml;den</I>), (iii) any consequential damages (<I>Folgesch&auml;den</I>), in particular
lost profits (<I>entgangener Gewinn</I>) or lost opportunities (<I>entgangene Gesch&auml;ftschancen</I>), (iv) any damages / losses to
good will, (v) any frustrated expenses (<I>vergebliche Aufwendungen</I>), as well as (vi) any internal administrative or overhead costs
or expenses incurred by the Purchaser, or any Target Group Company.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">Further, in case of a Breach, but
without prejudice to Section 8.4 a.), the Purchaser may not claim that the Purchase Price was calculated based (i) on incorrect assumptions
or economic parameters or (ii) on a wrong valuation of the Inpixon Shares and/or the business operations of the Target Group Companies
or a wrong valuation method applied (in particular based on a wrong multiple, multiplicators, <I>etc</I>.).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">Any payment by the Seller pursuant
to this Section&nbsp;8 shall be deemed as a subsequent reduction of the Purchase Price.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">8.2.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Limitations of Liability</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(1)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Seller&rsquo;s aggregate liability for any and all claims arising out of or in connection with any
Breach of the Seller&rsquo;s Warranties (other than the Seller&rsquo;s Warranties set out in Sections&nbsp;7.1 and 7.2 and the Tax Indemnity
in Section&nbsp;10) shall be limited to fifty percent (50% of the remaining unpaid balance of the Purchase Agreement).</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(2)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Seller shall not be liable for any individual claim unless the loss relating to such claim exceeds
EUR 15,000 (in words: Euro fifteen thousand) (<I>de minimis</I>). The Seller shall only be liable for claims once the aggregate amount
of all claims exceeding the de minimis exceeds EUR 100,000 (in words: Euro one hundred thousand) (<I>basket</I>), in which case the Seller
shall be liable for the amount exceeding the basket.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(3)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The aggregate liability of the Seller for any Breach of the warranties under Sections&nbsp;7.1 and 7.2
shall be limited to an amount being equal to 100% of the Purchase Price pursuant to Section&nbsp;4.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">8.3.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Time limitation</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">Any and all claims of the Purchaser
towards the Seller arising out of or in connection with this Agreement shall be time-barred (<I>verj&auml;hren</I>) at the earlier of
(i) twenty-four (24) months as of the Signing Date, except for claims arising out or in connection with a Breach of a Seller&rsquo;s Warranties
under Sections&nbsp;7.1 and 7.2, which shall be time-barred five (5) years after the Signing Date and (ii) claims arising from the Tax
Indemnity in Section&nbsp;10.2, which shall become time-barred in accordance with Section&nbsp;10.7. Sec.&nbsp;203&nbsp;BGB shall not
apply.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">8.4.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Excluded Items</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">The Seller shall not be liable for,
and the Purchaser shall not be entitled to claim for, any damages incurred by the Purchaser under or in connection with a Seller&rsquo;s Warranty
made in Section&nbsp;7, if and to the extent that:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">a.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">the fact, upon which the claim is based, is explicitly included in the Financial Statements, in particular,
but not limited to, as a write-off (<I>Abschreibung</I>), value adjustment (<I>Wertberichtigung</I>), specific provision (<I>R&uuml;ckstellung</I>),
liability (<I>Verbindlichkeit</I>) or general adjustment (<I>Pauschalwertberichtigung</I>);</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">b.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">any damages for which the Purchaser and/or any Target Group Company has received or has a valid and recoverable
claim for repayment, reimbursement, coverage or indemnification from a third party, including, but not limited to, claims against existing
insurance carriers, or any other benefit. The principle of set-off of benefits and damages (<I>Vorteilsausgleich</I>) pursuant to section
252 BGB shall apply;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">c.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">damages which occurred or increased due to changes in any law, other regulation, case law or administrative
practice after the Signing Date.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">8.5.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Disclosed Matters</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">8.5.1.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Exclusion of liability in case of Purchaser&acute;s knowledge</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">The Seller shall not be liable for,
and the Purchaser shall not be entitled to bring any claim under a Seller&rsquo;s Warranty, if and to the extent that the underlying facts or
circumstances giving rise to a Breach were known (<I>Kenntnis</I>) to the Purchaser or its direct or indirect shareholders at the Signing
Date.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">8.5.2.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Exclusion of liability in case of Purchaser&acute;s deemed knowledge</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">The following facts and circumstances
are deemed to be known by the Purchaser as of the Signing Date, irrespective of Purchaser actual knowledge thereof:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">a.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">all matters and information disclosed, contained or referred to in this Agreement, including its Schedules;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">b.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">answers, information and documents provided by or on behalf of the Seller during the Q&amp;A Process or
otherwise in writing;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">c.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">all matters and information disclosed, provided for or noted in the Financial Statements and/or the Proforma
Management Accounts; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">d.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">all matters and information disclosed to the Purchaser, any of the Purchaser&rsquo;s or direct or indirect
shareholders at any presentations by and meetings with the management of the Target Group Companies.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">8.5.3.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>No Knowledge of Claims</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">The Purchaser confirms that the Purchaser
is not aware of any fact or circumstances that could constitute a Breach of a Seller&rsquo;s Warranty or could otherwise give rise to any claim
under this Agreement.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">8.6.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>No double-dip</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">The Parties agree that where one and
the same set of facts (<I>Sachverhalt</I>) qualifies under more than one provision entitling the Purchaser to a claim or remedy under
this Agreement or any applicable statutory laws, there shall be only one claim or remedy (no double-dip).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">8.7.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Notification of a Breach of Warranty</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">In the event of a Breach of a Seller&rsquo;s
Warranty pursuant to Section&nbsp;7 that may give rise to liability of the Seller under the terms of this Agreement, the Purchaser shall
notify the Seller of such Breach without undue delay (<I>unverz&uuml;glich</I>) after becoming aware of the relevant circumstances of
the inaccuracy or potential Breach of Warranty in writing (the &ldquo;<B>Breach Notice&rdquo;</B>). The Breach Notice must contain a reasonably
detailed description of the potential Breach of Warranty and the Purchaser&rsquo;s potential claim arising therefrom, including the estimated
amount of such claim, and the Purchaser shall give the Seller the opportunity to cure the breach within the period of time indicated in
Section&nbsp;8.1 above.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">8.8.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Third Party Claim</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">In the event that any action, claim,
demand or proceeding with respect to which the Purchaser may request indemnification pursuant to Section&nbsp;8 is asserted or announced
against any Target Group Company or the Purchaser by any third party (including any tax or governmental authority) (a &ldquo;<B>Third
Party Claim&rdquo;</B>), the Purchaser shall notify the Seller thereof by way of a Breach Notice and provide the Seller with copies of
documents setting forth the Third Party Claim or demand and of all time-sensitive documents. Neither the Purchaser nor any Target Group
Company shall make any admission of liability, agreement or compromise in relation to any Third-Party Claim without the prior written
consent of the Seller.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">a.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Seller will be afforded a reasonable opportunity to resist any Third Party Claim in the name of the
Purchaser or the relevant Target Group Company, and the Seller will be allowed to have the conduct of any negotiations, proceedings, or
appeals relating to any Third Party Claim and to use professional advisors nominated by the Seller. The costs and expenses incurred by
Seller in connection with any defense against a Third Party Claim will be borne by Seller.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">b.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Purchaser or the Target Group Companies shall at all reasonable times allow the Seller access to and
to inspect, take and retain copies of, all relevant business records and documents, and permit the Seller and its representatives to consult
with the directors, officers, employees and representatives of the Purchaser and the Target Group Companies. The costs and expenses incurred
by the Seller in connection with any defense against a Third Party Claim will be borne by the Seller.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">c.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Purchaser shall be responsible for (<I>einstehen</I>) and ensure that the Target Group Companies fully
comply with their obligations under this Section&nbsp;8.8.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">8.9.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Mitigation</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">Section 254 BGB shall apply. The Purchaser
shall in particular be obliged to prevent the occurrence of any damages and to limit the scope of any damages incurred.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">8.10.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>No further rights and claims of the Purchaser</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(1)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Parties agree that the liability regime for a Breach of a Seller&rsquo;s Warranty set forth in this Agreement
shall be the sole and only remedy to any Breach of a Seller&rsquo;s Warranty, if any, except for any liability of the Seller due to intentional
behaviour (<I>Vorsatz</I>) or fraud (<I>T&auml;uschung</I>).</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(2)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">To the extent permitted by law, the Parties agree that all further rights and claims of the Purchaser
against the Seller based on material or legal defects (<I>Sach- und Rechtsm&auml;ngeln</I>) of the Inpixon Shares, the Aware Shares or
the IntraNav Shares or the Target Group Companies&rsquo; business &ndash; irrespective of their nature, amount or legal basis &ndash;
are hereby excluded, including any rights and claims based on defects of the Company&rsquo;s business, unless such rights and claims are
based on intentional behaviour (<I>Vorsatz)</I> or fraud (<I>T&auml;uschung</I>) of the Seller. The Parties exclude any claims for breach
of a pre-contractual duty (Sec. 311 para. 2 and 3, 241 para. 2 BGB), claims based on a breach of duty in an obligation relationship (<I>Verletzung
einer Pflicht aus dem Schuldverh&auml;ltnis</I>), claims based on statutory warranty provisions (<I>gesetzliche Gew&auml;hrleistungsbestimmungen</I>)
and liability in tort (<I>unerlaubte Handlung</I>) as well as any and all other claims which could, due to a rescission (<I>R&uuml;cktritt</I>),
action for avoidance (<I>Anfechtung</I>), reduction of the Purchase Price (<I>Minderung</I>) or other reasons, result in the termination
(<I>Beendigung</I>), invalidity (<I>Unwirksamkeit</I>) or a winding-up or restitution ex tunc (<I>R&uuml;ckabwicklung</I>) of this Agreement,
in an amendment of its content or in a refund or reduction of the Purchase Price.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(1)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">For a period of two (2) years after the Signing Date, the Seller shall not, neither directly nor indirectly,
and the Seller shall procure that none of its Affiliates shall</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">a.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">engage in any business competing with the business of the Target Group Companies as conducted as of the
Signing Date, acquire or hold any interest in a competing business or advise or assist any competing business, save for any financial

only and in which the Seller does not have, directly or indirectly, a management function or any material influence on the conduct of
business.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(3)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Parties agree that in the event of a breach by the Seller of the non-compete obligation under Section&nbsp;9.1
above, the Purchaser shall be entitled to enforce any claims for specific performance by the Seller of the non-compete obligation (<I>Unterlassungs-
und Beseitigungsanspr&uuml;che</I>) by injunctive relief (<I>einstweiliger Rechtsschutz</I>).</TD></TR></TABLE>

Operating Capital and shall be subject to the limitations set forth in Section 4.2.3(b):</P>

as described in such 2025 PO. The Parties acknowledge that in order to deliver Products pursuant to the 2025 PO, Inpixon contracted with
Bluechips Microhouse - Electronic Manufacturing Services, a contract manufacturer in Chaing Mai, Thailand (the &ldquo;<B>Contract Manufacturer</B>&rdquo;),
to assemble the Products and drop ship such Products to Arrow Electronics as provided in the 2025 PO. In order for Contract Manufacturer
to assemble the Products, prior to the Closing Date, Inpixon ordered certain components necessary for the assembly of such &ldquo;<B>Ordered
Components</B>&rdquo;. Inpixon will be responsible for causing the assembly of the Products including the Ordered Components and the Products
are to be inspected by Inpixon personnel prior to shipment to Arrow Electronics. The Seller, however, has agreed that the costs of such
Ordered Components either have been or will be absorbed and paid for by Seller. The Seller indemnifies the Purchaser and the relevant
Target Group Company from all costs and expenses relating to such Ordered Components. The Seller has left and will leave all proceeds
from the 2025 PO in Inpixon; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">10.1.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Definitions</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">For the purposes of this Agreement
the following terms, shall have the following meaning:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&ldquo;<B>Shareholder Loan Tax Cap</B>&rdquo;
means an amount equal to <B>USD 2,500,000</B>, representing the maximum aggregate liability of the Seller under this Agreement in respect
of all Taxes arising in Germany as a result of, or in connection with, the pre-Closing waiver, contribution, cancellation, or other elimination
of all or any portion of the Shareholder Loan and any related intercompany balances, including any taxable income resulting from any portion
thereof being treated as non-substantiated (in German: <I>nicht werthaltig</I>) for German tax purposes.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&ldquo;<B>Taxes&rdquo;</B> means all
direct and indirect taxes and withholding taxes within the meaning of Section 3 para. 1 of the German Tax Code (<I>AO</I>), social security
and pension contributions, customs duties, and any similar assessments or charges imposed by any competent governmental authority or public
body in charge of imposing any Tax (collectively, the &ldquo;<B>Tax Authorities</B>&rdquo;), pursuant to the applicable law of any other
jurisdiction , in each case together with any interest, penalties, surcharges and additions and irrespective of whether the aforementioned
levies are owed primarily (including withholding taxes), as a consequence of any statutory secondary liability (e.g. due to Section 75
AO) or are owed as a consequence of any contractual liability (e.g. due to a tax sharing or tax indemnity agreement) or of any other civil
law liability, but excluding deferred taxes and/or notional taxes (such as reductions of loss carry forwards or future depreciation);</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify"><B>&ldquo;Tax Return&rdquo;</B> shall
mean any return, declaration or similar document relating to any Tax and submitted or to be submitted to any Tax Authority, including
any schedule or attachment thereto;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify"></P>

<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">e.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">neither the German Target Group Companies, nor the Purchaser nor any of its Affiliates has (or had at
any time following the Signing Date) a corresponding claim for recourse, repayment or indemnification against a third party or could have
been compensated by such claim, but was not so compensated, because of any non-compliance with the preconditions for such claim for recourse,
repayment or indemnification; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">f.)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">neither the German Target Group Companies, nor the Purchaser nor any of its Affiliates has failed to comply
in total or in parts with any of its obligations set forth in Section&nbsp;10.6 unless and to the extent the Purchaser proves that the
non-compliance has not caused or increased and neither excluded or substantially impaired the Seller&rsquo;s ability to defend or avoid the
Indemnifiable Taxes.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(2)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">In case of Section 10.2(b) the Purchaser after the Closing has taken and will take, to the extent commercially
reasonable and consistent with the ordinary-course operation of the German Target Group Companies, reasonable steps to mitigate any Taxes.
Any indemnification payments under Section&nbsp;10.2 to the extend not limited by Section&nbsp;10.3 by the Seller shall be made sixty
(60) Business Days after the date at which the Seller has been notified in writing by the Purchaser about the payment obligation and has
been provided with a copy of the relevant Tax assessment notice, but in no case earlier than five (5) Business Days prior to the date
at which the Indemnifiable Tax is due and payable to the Tax Authority. On the Seller&rsquo;s written request and expense, the Purchaser shall
procure that German Target Group Companies undertake best efforts to achieve a deferred payment date, in particular, but not limited to,
the application for a suspension of enforcement of the Tax payment obligation (<I>Aussetzung der Vollziehung</I>) under German tax laws
or equivalent application in a foreign jurisdiction. If an Indemnifiable Tax is reduced after an indemnification payment has been made,
the difference between the higher indemnification payment and the lower Tax amount shall be reimbursed by the Purchaser to the Seller,
including all interest relating thereto; any respective payment to the Seller shall be due within twenty (20) Business Days after the
date at which the German Target Group Companies have received the respective amount from the relevant Tax Authority (including by way
of set-off, deduction or otherwise).</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">10.4.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Tax Refunds and Overprovisions</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">(1)</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">The Purchaser shall pay to the Seller the amount of a refund (including
interest thereon) of Taxes relating to any Tax periods (or parts of a Tax period) up to and including December 31, 2025, which exceeds
the amount of the Tax receivables included in the Financial Statements for Taxes (the &ldquo;<B>Tax Refund&rdquo;</B></FONT>)<FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">).
Any such payment shall be due and payable within twenty (20) Business Days after such Tax Refund has been received by any German Target
Group Company by cash payment, set-off, deduction or otherwise.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">(2)</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">The Purchaser shall promptly pay to the Seller an amount equal to any Tax
liabilities and Tax accruals and provisions included, also as part of other liabilities, accruals and provisions, in the Financial Statements,
if and to the extent it turns out that such liabilities, accruals or provisions can be dissolved as overstated after December 31, 2025
pursuant to the applicable statutory accounting principles, unless such liabilities, accruals or provisions have excluded a Tax Indemnification
Claim pursuant to Section&nbsp;10.3 (1) a (the &ldquo;<B>Overprovision&rdquo;</B></FONT>)<FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">).</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(3)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Purchaser shall, and shall procure (<I>steht daf&uuml;r ein</I>) that the German Target Group Companies,
(i) promptly notify the Seller in writing of (A) the receipt (including, but not limited to, by way of set-off or deduction) of any Tax
Refund and (B) the occurrence of any Overprovision and (ii) upon the Seller&rsquo;s written request deliver to the Seller within six (6) months
following such request a written statement of a reputable audit firm (<I>Wirtschaftspr&uuml;fungsgesellschaft</I>) nominated by the Seller
confirming that the Purchaser has fully complied with these notification obligations, including a confirmation of the notified amounts.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">10.5.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Tax Covenant</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">The Purchaser shall ensure that, except
as required by applicable law or by any binding request or order of a Tax Authority, and after having given the Seller the opportunity
to intervene, neither the Purchaser nor any of the Target Group Companies will on or after the Signing Date take any action, make or change
any Tax election, amend any Tax Return, take a Tax position, undertake or omit to undertake any action or enter into any transaction,
merger or restructuring in relation to the German Target Group Companies that results in an increase of Taxes imposed on the Seller unless
otherwise directed by Seller and/or Seller&rsquo;s tax professionals. If the Purchaser fails to comply with such obligation or the obligations
set out in Section&nbsp;10.6 the Purchaser shall indemnify the Seller from and against any (additional) Taxes resulting therefrom, unless
that the Purchaser&rsquo;s failure has neither prejudiced the Seller to defend nor mitigate such (additional) Taxes.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">10.6.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Cooperation on Tax Matters</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(1)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">After the Signing Date, the Purchaser shall procure that the German Target Group Companies (i) amend their
respective 2023 and 2024 Tax Returns, and (ii) prepare and file when due all Tax Returns relating to any Tax periods (or parts of a Tax
period) up to and including December 31, 2025, and (iii) prepare their 2025 and 2026 Tax Return, with each of the 2023 and 2024 amendments
and the 2025 and 2026 Tax Returns being amended and prepared, as the case may be, in a manner and to the extent requested or directed
by Seller and/or Seller&rsquo;s tax professionals to minimize the tax impact of the Shareholder Loan Waiver. Further, Purchaser shall
cause the German Target Group Companies to also prepare their respective 2026 Tax Return reflecting income relative to the Shareholder
Loan Waiver as directed by Seller&rsquo;s professionals. Failure of the Purchaser and the German Target Group Companies to comply with
this Section shall cause the Shareholder Loan Tax Cap to be automatically reduced to zero. Any annual Tax Returns relating to such (especially
2023, 2024, 2025 and 2026) Tax periods shall be subject to the review and written consent of the Seller. The Purchaser shall not, and
shall procure that the German Target Group Companies will not, submit any such annual Tax Return to any Tax Authority without such prior
review and written approval by the Seller, which shall not be unreasonably withheld, conditioned or delayed. The Purchaser shall ensure
that any draft annual Tax Return to be reviewed and approved by the Seller in writing will be sent to the Seller not later than thirty
(30) Business Days prior to the due filing date of the relevant Tax Return. The Purchaser will without unreasonable delay provide any
information which the Seller deems to be relevant for the review of the draft Tax Return.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">(2)</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">The Purchaser shall notify the Seller of any announcement, commencement
or enforcement of any Tax Proceedings relating to any Tax periods (or parts of a Tax period) up to and including December 31, 2025 (the
&ldquo;<B>Relevant Tax Proceedings&rdquo; </B></FONT>) <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">promptly and in any event no later than ten (10) Business
Days after the Purchaser and / or the German Target Group Companies had been informed of such event. The notification shall be made in
writing and shall contain necessary information describing the object of the Relevant Tax Proceeding and shall include copies of any Tax
assessment notice or other document received from any Tax Authority. Upon the Seller&rsquo;s request, the Purchaser shall procure that the Seller
obtain any available additional document or information (including any books and records) which the Seller reasonably deems to be relevant
in this respect.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(3)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Purchaser shall, and shall cause the German Target Group Companies to, (i) ensure that to the extent
permitted by law the Seller is given the opportunity to fully participate in (including the participation in all meetings and other conversations
with the Tax Authorities) any Relevant Tax Proceedings which take place after the Signing Date, (ii) upon the Seller&rsquo;s written request
and expense file objections or other appeals against Tax assessments or challenge and litigate any Tax assessment or other decision of
any Tax Authority and (iii) comply with any lawful instructions given by the Seller in relation to the conduct of the Relevant Tax Proceedings.
If the Seller elects to lead a Relevant Tax Proceeding on its own or through a counsel of its own choice, the Purchaser shall authorize,
and shall cause the German Target Group Companies to authorize, the designated representative of the Seller to represent the Purchaser
and / or the German Target Group Companies in the Relevant Tax Proceeding. In any case, the Purchaser shall not, and shall cause the German
Target Group Companies not to furnish any information relating to any Relevant Tax Proceedings or settle any Relevant Tax Proceeding or
to let them become time-barred without the prior written consent of the Seller, which shall not be unreasonably withheld, conditioned
or delayed.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">10.7.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Time Limitation</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">Any claims under this Section&nbsp;10
shall not become time-barred prior to the expiration of a period of six (6) months after the respective Tax assessment for the relevant
Tax underlying the claim has become final and unappealable (<I>formell und materiell bestandskr&auml;ftig</I>), provided, however that
any claims of the Purchaser shall become time-barred at the latest five (5) years after the Signing Date.</P>

in this Agreement, claims arising out of or in connection with this Section&nbsp;10 shall be subject only to the limitations expressly
provided for in this Section&nbsp;10.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">Purchaser is acquiring the Inpixon
Shares and the Target Group Companies for its own account.</P>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">11.1.2.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Corporate Status and Authority</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">11.2.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Remedies of Seller</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">In the event that the Purchaser is
in breach of any warranty pursuant to Section&nbsp;11.1 above, the Purchaser shall indemnify and hold harmless the Seller from and against
any damages incurred by the Seller. The limitation period for any claims of the Seller shall be twelve (12) months as of the Signing Date.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">12.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Purchaser&rsquo;s Undertaking</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">12.1.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Subordination of Claims</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">In order to avoid over-indebtedness
or any other reason for insolvency on the part of Inpixon, the Purchaser undertakes towards the Seller to subordinate, and to uphold such
subordination during the Unwind Option Exercise Period, all current and future claims arising from funding granted by the Purchaser to
the Target Group Companies, including repayment claims of such funding. The Purchaser&rsquo;s claims against Inpixon arising from funding by
Purchaser to the Target Group Companies may only be settled from future profits, any liquidation surplus, or from free assets exceeding
the company&rsquo;s other liabilities, after all company creditors within the meaning of section 39 (2) InsO have been satisfied and on an equal
footing with the shareholders&rsquo; claims for repayment of contributions within the meaning of section 199 sentence 2 InsO (<I>Qualifizierter
Rangr&uuml;cktritt</I>).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">All disputes arising out of or in
connection with this Arbitration or its validity shall be finally settled in accordance with the Arbitration Rules of the German Arbitration
Institute e.V. (DIS) without recourse to the ordinary courts of law. The arbitral tribunal shall comprise three (3) arbitrators. The place
of arbitration shall be D&uuml;sseldorf, Germany. The language of the arbitral proceedings shall be English. This shall not prevent the
Parties from asserting any claims under this Agreement against the other Party by seeking injunctive relief before the competent courts.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">This Agreement represents the entire
understanding and agreement between the Parties with respect to its subject matter and supersedes all prior agreements, understandings,
negotiations and communications relating to such subject matter unless otherwise specifically stated in this Agreement. Neither Party
shall be liable to the other Party or to any third party for any promise, representation, warranty, covenant, provision or practice except
as specifically stated in this Agreement.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">15.5.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><U>Amendments and Waivers</U></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">Any amendment to or waiver of this
Agreement shall be made in writing and shall have no effect before signed by the duly authorized representatives of both Parties or, in
the case of a waiver, by the Party waiving compliance with this Agreement, unless more stringent form requirements (e.g. notarization)
must be satisfied under applicable law.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">Failure by any Party at any time to
require performance of any provisions of this Agreement shall in no manner affect its right to enforce the same, and the waiver by any
Party of any breach of any provision of this Agreement shall not be construed to be a waiver by such Party of any succeeding breach of
such provision or waiver by such Party of any breach of any other provision hereof.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">This Agreement and the rights and
obligations specified hereunder shall be binding upon and inure to the benefit of the Parties and shall not be assignable by either Party
without the prior written consent of the other Party.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 28.35pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B><I>RECITALS</I></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>WHEREAS,
</B></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">on or about November 7, 2016 Employee entered into that certain Employment
Agreement (the <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><I>&ldquo;<B>Original Employment Agreement&rdquo;</B></I>) </FONT>with Sysorex USA <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">(<I>&ldquo;<B>Sysorex</B>&rdquo;</I>),
</FONT>which such Original Employment Agreement was amended as of August 31, 2018 by instrument executed by Employee, Sysorex, and Inpixon,
Inc., a Nevada corporation <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">(<I>&ldquo;<B>Inpixon</B>&rdquo;</I></FONT> which was by such time the parent
of Sysorex) (the <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><I>&ldquo;<B>Amendment</B>&rdquo;</I>) </FONT>whereupon Employee became an employee of
Inpixon; and</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0.5in; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>WHEREAS,
</B></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">on March 11, 2024, Inpixon and XTI Aircraft Company, a Delaware corporation
<FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">(<I>&ldquo;<B>Aircraft</B>&rdquo;</I>) </FONT>entered into a transaction pursuant to which (the <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><I>&ldquo;<B>Merger</B>&rdquo;</I>)
</FONT>pursuant to which Inpixon was the surviving entity, (i) changed its name to XTI Aerospace Inc., (ii) XTI Aircraft Company became
a wholly-owned subsidiary of XTI, (iii) XTI inherited two German subsidiaries: (x) Inpixon GmbH, (y) IntraNav GmbH, based in Eschborn,
Germany, an indirect subsidiary of XTI (collectively, the <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">(<I>&ldquo;<B>Inpixon Companies</B>&rdquo;</I>),
</FONT>with the German Companies comprising the entire business unit of XTI generally referred to as Inpixon focused on real-time location
systems <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">(<I>&ldquo;<B>RTLS</B>&rsquo;&rsquo;</I>) </FONT>technology providing location intelligence solutions
in factories and other industrial facilities to help optimize operations, increase productivity, and enhance safety (the <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><I>&ldquo;<B>Inpixon
Business&rdquo;</B></I>);</FONT> and</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0.5in; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>WHEREAS,
</B></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">in addition, in connection with the Merger, and as of the time of
such Merger, <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">(i) </FONT>Employee became the Chief Executive Officer of Inpixon and was appointed to the
Board of Directors of XTI (the <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B><I>&ldquo;Board&rsquo;&rsquo;</I></B>), <I></I></FONT>and (ii) Employee&rsquo;s
Base Salary and Bonus as initially described in the Original Employment Agreement, were amended such that, through Inpixon, Employees
Base Salary and Bonus were, immediately prior to the Effective Date hereof, as follows:</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0.5in; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-indent: 1in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Base
Salary: $312,000 (Employee&rsquo;s <B><I>&ldquo;Current Base Salary&rdquo;</I></B>)</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-indent: 1in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-indent: 1in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Bonus:
$300,000 (Employee&rsquo;s <B><I>&ldquo;Current Bonus&rdquo;</I></B>); <B></B>and</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0.5in; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>WHEREAS,
</B></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Employee following the Merger awarded certain stock options to acquire
the Company&rsquo;s common stock (generally, the <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B><I>&ldquo;Options&rdquo; </I></B></FONT>to acquire

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>WHEREAS,</B>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>NOW,
THEREFORE, </B>incorporating herein the foregoing Recitals, and for good and valuable consideration, the Parties agree, as follows:</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0.5in; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1<I>.<B>&nbsp;</B></I><B>Board
Resignation. </B>Employee hereby resigns from and shall cease to serve as a member of the Company&rsquo;s Board as of the Board Resignation
Date (generally the <B><I>&ldquo;Board Resignation&rdquo;</I></B>).</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0.5in; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.<B><I>&nbsp;</I>Resignation
from all other Positions as of the Effective Date. </B>Employee does hereby tender Employee&rsquo;s resignation as Chief Executive
Officer of Inpixon and from any and all other positions Employee holds with any of the XTI Companies, as of the Effective Date
(generally the <B><I>&ldquo;XTI Resignation&rdquo; </I></B>and together with the Board Resignation, the <B><I>&ldquo;Resignations.</I></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">3<I>.</I><B>&nbsp;Public
Announcement. </B>Except as may be required by regulatory or legal requirement, the Company will not make any public announcement concerning
Employee&rsquo;s XTI Resignation.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0.5in; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

Companies, as of the Effective Date.</FONT></P>

complete satisfaction of any and all amounts the Company or any of the XTI Companies or the Inpixon Companies may owe to Employee,
or Employee&rsquo;s heirs, representatives, and/or assigns, up to and through the Effective Date, including, but not limited to (x)

Employee&rsquo;s employment with any of the XTI Companies, and/or (y) any amounts Employee may in any way be entitled to under the

agrees, as follows:</FONT></P>

orientation, gender identification or on any other legally protected basis. Employee understands and agrees that he has no claim for

or any of the Company Releasees as defined below, asserting any claims that are released in this Agreement.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">16.<B>&nbsp;<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: underline solid">Confidentiality
of this Agreement</FONT>. </B>The Parties shall keep the facts and terms of this Agreement confidential, and not to disclose such information
to anyone other than to that Party&rsquo;s own spouse, if any, attorneys and the Company&rsquo;s board of directors, management team
and others within the Company with a need to know such information (hereafter referred to as <I>&ldquo;<B>Parties&rsquo; Confidants</B>&rdquo;</I>),
<I></I>all of whom will be informed of and be bound by this confidentiality provision. Unless otherwise required by a governmental authority,
neither of the Parties nor the Parties&rsquo; Confidants shall disclose the facts, amount or terms of this Agreement to anyone including,
but not limited to, any Internet or Internet media, any print, radio or television media, to any past, present or prospective applicant
for employment with the Company, to any current or former employee of the Company, to any counsel for any current or former employee
of the Company, to any other counsel or third party, or to the public at large. The Parties understand and agree that any disclosure
of information in violation of this confidentiality provision by a Party or by any of Parties&rsquo; Confidants would cause injury and
damage, the actual amount of which would be impractical or extremely difficult to determine. Accordingly, the Parties agree that any
Party shall be entitled to an immediate injunction and then shall be entitled to equitable relief as well as whatever legal damages suffered.
If any proceeding is brought concerning an alleged violation of this confidentiality provision, the prevailing Party shall recover from
the losing Party all reasonable attorneys&rsquo; fees and costs incurred in connection with such proceeding. The non breaching Party
shall have the burden of proving by a preponderance of the evidence such violation by the breaching Party.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">17.<B>&nbsp;<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: underline solid">Successors</FONT>.
</B>This Agreement shall be binding upon the Parties and their respective heirs, administrators, representatives, executors, successors
and assigns, and shall inure to the benefit of the Company Releasees and the Employee Releasees.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">18.<B>&nbsp;<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: underline solid">Mediation</FONT>. </B>The
Parties to this Agreement agree to mediate any dispute or claim arising out of or relating to this Agreement or any resulting
transaction therefrom, including selection of forum of the dispute, before resorting to court action, subject to exclusions from
mediation as set forth. The Parties shall agree upon a mediator mutually acceptable to them and mediation fees, if any, shall be
divided equally among the Parties involved. If any Party commences an action based on the dispute or claim to which this Paragraph
applies, without first attempting to resolve the matter through mediation, then that Party shall not be entitled to recover
attorneys&rsquo; fees, even if they would otherwise be available to that Party in any such action. Should Employee or the Company
institute any legal action or administrative proceeding with respect to any claim waived by this Agreement or pursue any dispute or
matter covered by this paragraph by any method other than said mediation, the responding Party shall be entitled to recover from the
other Party all damages, costs, expenses and attorneys&rsquo; fees incurred as a result of such action. The only exception to this
clause regarding mediating disputes shall be a claim for injunctive relief for disclosure or threatened disclosure of Trade Secrets,
as described </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">in <FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">this
Agreement.</FONT></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">19.<B>&nbsp;<FONT STYLE="text-decoration: underline solid">Mutual
Non-Disparagement</FONT>. </B>The Parties are executing this Agreement on an amicable basis and both parties agree to speak favorably
about the other. The Parties further agree not to falsely or maliciously disparage one another, and their officers, directors, employees,
shareholders and agents, in any manner likely to be harmful to them or their business, business reputation or personal reputation; provided
that the Parties may respond accurately and fully to any request for information if required by legal process or in connection with a
government investigation. In addition, nothing in this provision or this Agreement is intended to prohibit or restrain either Party in
any manner from making disclosures that are protected under the whistleblower provisions of federal law or regulation or under other
applicable law or regulation.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
